dat = read.csv("Advertising.csv")
head(dat)
names(dat)[names(dat) == "ï..TV"] <- "TV"

# Check the updated column names
names(dat)
[1] "TV"        "Radio"     "Newspaper" "Sales"

model-1: Sales~TV

## why R-sq is not good
add one more variable with random values


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuYGBgclxuc2V0LnNlZWQoMDIwMSlcbnggPSBzYW1wbGUoMToyMDApXG54MiA9IHNhbXBsZSgxOjIwMClcbngzID0gc2FtcGxlKDE6MjAwKVxuXG5cbm0yID0gbG0oU2FsZXN+VFYreCt4Mit4MywgZGF0YSA9IGRhdClcbnN1bW1hcnkobTIpXG5gYGBcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
```r
set.seed(0201)
x = sample(1:200)
x2 = sample(1:200)
x3 = sample(1:200)


m2 = lm(Sales~TV+x+x2+x3, data = dat)
summary(m2)

### prediction

<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuYGBgclxubmV3X2RhdGEgPSBkYXRhLmZyYW1lKFxuICBUViA9IGMoMjAwLCAyNTApLFxuICBSYWRpbyA9IGMoMTAwLCA1MCksXG4gIE5ld3NwYXBlciA9IGMoMjAsIDUwKVxuKVxuICBcbnByZWRpY3QobW9kZWw0LCBuZXdkYXRhID0gbmV3X2RhdGEpXG5gYGBcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
```r
new_data = data.frame(
  TV = c(200, 250),
  Radio = c(100, 50),
  Newspaper = c(20, 50)
)
  
predict(model4, newdata = new_data)

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-chunk-end -->


<!-- rnb-text-begin -->

<!-- rnb-text-end -->
